nixpkgs / kotlin-native - Kotlin/Native is a technology for compiling Kotlin code to native binaries, which can run without a virtual machine. It is an LLVM based backend for the Kotlin compiler and native implementation of the Kotlin standard library.

Homepage - https://kotlinlang.org/

License - Apache-2.0
